Three things that can push a man to despair.

Va'kin: "I should've never let go of her that night.."
Luna: "Nearly got you killed..."

Abandoned by his mother: "Why......"

The faces of the many lives he's taken: "So many innocent people...."
Skeletons long since buried slowly crawling back and pulling him under.

He was a train wreck with no way out..Suffering from things he could never fix.
